INC-SOURCE (P-LI7) A Proton Beam of 98 MeV Impinged on a 200      2265900100020 
            mg/cm2 Thick Lithium Target, Enriched to 99.98%       2265900100021 
            In 7-Li. The Unaffected Proton Beam was Bent by       2265900100022 
            A Magnet Into a Well-Shielded Beam Dump, While the    2265900100023 
            Neutrons were Collimated in a Narrow Cone at 0 Degrees2265900100024 
            By a Heavy Collimator System, Before Entering the Ex- 2265900100025 
            Perimental Area About 8 M After the Production Target.2265900100026 
            The Neutron Beam Spot at the Irradiation Position had 2265900100027 
            A Diameter of 7 cm. With a 5 Microamp Beam, the Neu-  2265900100028 
            Tron Yield at That Position was About 1.0E+06 Neutrons2265900100029 
            Per Sec.                                              2265900100030 
INC-SPECT  .The Neutrons Showed a Semi-Monoenergetic Neutron Spec-2265900100031 
            Trum, with a Full Energy Peak and a Low-Energy Tail.  2265900100032 
            The Latter was Supressed by Tof and Unfolding Tech-   2265900100033 
            Niques.                                               2265900100034 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,SIG)                                2265900100035 
MONIT-REF  (,N.OLSSON+,C,94GATLIN,1,60,199405)  For (N,P) Sigma   2265900100036 
           (,ROENNQVIST+,J,PR/C,45,(2),496,199202)                2265900100037 
DETECTOR   (TELES,PROPC,PROPC)  Four Drift Chambers               2265900100038 
           (MAGSP) The Recoil Protons were Detected by a Magnetic 2265900100039 
            Spectrograph, Equipped with Four Position-Sensitive   2265900100040 
            Drift Chambers and Three Trigger Scintillators. The   2265900100041 
            Proton Energy and Emission Angle was Determined by    2265900100042 
            Ray-Tracing Through the Magnetic Field. The Energy    2265900100043 
            Resolution of the Spectrometer was About 3.5 MeV Fwhm 2265900100044 
            In the Angular Range 0-15 Degrees, and 4.5 MeV Fwhm in2265900100045 
            The Angular Range 15-30 Degrees.                      2265900100046 
           (MWPC )                                                2265900100047 
           (SCIN )                                                2265900100048 
METHOD     (TOF)                                                  2265900100049

SAMPLE      .A Sandwiched Multitarget System was Used.            2265900100051 
            It Consisted of a Stack of Thin (N,P)Target Foil      2265900100052 
            Interspaced by Multiwire Proportional Chambers.       2265900100053 
            Efficiency Per Chamber Plane is Above 99%             2265900100054 
           .Isotopically Enriched to More Than 99% B-10 and       2265900100055 
            B-11 Powder was Mixed with Water to a Mud Which was   2265900100056 
            Then Dried on a Polypropilene Foil As Backing.        2265900100057 
            Second Such Foil was Mounted to Seal the Boron Sample 2265900100058 
           .Two Samples of B-10 were Mounted in the First Two     2265900100059 
            Positions of the Multitarget Box Having 226 and 287   2265900100060 
            mg/cm2 Thickness. In the Following Positions Three    2265900100061 
            B-11 Samples 243, 248, 290 mg/cm2 Thick were Mounted  2265900100062 
           .A 102 mg/cm2 C-H2 Reference Foilwas Placed in the Last2265900100063 
            Target Position                                       2265900100064
